_ltmatrix() {
    local i cur prev opts cmd
    COMPREPLY=()
    if [[ "${BASH_VERSINFO[0]}" -ge 4 ]]; then
        cur="$2"
    else
        cur="${COMP_WORDS[COMP_CWORD]}"
    fi
    prev="$3"
    cmd=""
    opts=""

    for i in "${COMP_WORDS[@]:0:COMP_CWORD}"
    do
        case "${cmd},${i}" in
            ",$1")
                cmd="ltmatrix"
                ;;
            ltmatrix,cleanup)
                cmd="ltmatrix__cleanup"
                ;;
            ltmatrix,completions)
                cmd="ltmatrix__completions"
                ;;
            ltmatrix,help)
                cmd="ltmatrix__help"
                ;;
            ltmatrix,man)
                cmd="ltmatrix__man"
                ;;
            ltmatrix,release)
                cmd="ltmatrix__release"
                ;;
            ltmatrix__help,cleanup)
                cmd="ltmatrix__help__cleanup"
                ;;
            ltmatrix__help,completions)
                cmd="ltmatrix__help__completions"
                ;;
            ltmatrix__help,help)
                cmd="ltmatrix__help__help"
                ;;
            ltmatrix__help,man)
                cmd="ltmatrix__help__man"
                ;;
            ltmatrix__help,release)
                cmd="ltmatrix__help__release"
                ;;
            *)
                ;;
        esac
    done

    case "${cmd}" in
        ltmatrix)
            opts="-c -h -V --agent --mode --fast --expert --config --output --log-level --log-file --max-retries --timeout --dry-run --resume --ask --regenerate-plan --on-blocked --mcp-config --no-color --help --version [GOAL] release completions man cleanup help"
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 1 ]] ; then
                COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                --agent)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                --mode)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W "fast standard expert" -- "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                --config)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                -c)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                --output)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W "text json json-compact" -- "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                --log-level)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W "trace debug info warn error" -- "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                --log-file)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                --max-retries)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                --timeout)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                --on-blocked)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W "skip ask abort retry" -- "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                --mcp-config)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                *)
                    COMPREPLY=()
                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
            return 0
            ;;
        ltmatrix__cleanup)
            opts="-h --reset-all --reset-failed --remove --force --dry-run --no-color --help"
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 2 ]] ; then
                COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                *)
                    COMPREPLY=()
                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
            return 0
            ;;
        ltmatrix__completions)
            opts="-h --install --no-color --help bash zsh fish powershell elvish"
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 2 ]] ; then
                COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                *)
                    COMPREPLY=()
                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
            return 0
            ;;
        ltmatrix__help)
            opts="release completions man cleanup help"
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 2 ]] ; then
                COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                *)
                    COMPREPLY=()
                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
            return 0
            ;;
        ltmatrix__help__cleanup)
            opts=""
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 3 ]] ; then
                COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                *)
                    COMPREPLY=()
                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )

        ltmatrix__help__completions)

                *)
                    COMPREPLY=()

            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )

        ltmatrix__help__help)
            opts=""
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 3 ]] ; then

            case "${prev}" in

                    COMPREPLY=()

            esac

                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                *)
                    COMPREPLY=()
                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
            return 0
            ;;
        ltmatrix__man)
            opts="-o -h --output --no-color --help"
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 2 ]] ; then
                COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                --output)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                -o)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                *)
                    COMPREPLY=()
                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
            return 0
            ;;
        ltmatrix__release)
            opts="-h --target --output --archive --all-targets --no-color --help"
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 2 ]] ; then
                COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                --target)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0

                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0

                    COMPREPLY=()
                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
            return 0
            ;;
    esac
}

_ltmatrix() {
    local i cur prev opts cmd
    COMPREPLY=()
    if [[ "${BASH_VERSINFO[0]}" -ge 4 ]]; then
        cur="$2"
    else
        cur="${COMP_WORDS[COMP_CWORD]}"
    fi
    prev="$3"
    cmd=""
    opts=""

    for i in "${COMP_WORDS[@]:0:COMP_CWORD}"
    do
        case "${cmd},${i}" in
            ",$1")
                cmd="ltmatrix"
                ;;
            ltmatrix,cleanup)
                cmd="ltmatrix__cleanup"
                ;;
            ltmatrix,completions)
                cmd="ltmatrix__completions"
                ;;
            ltmatrix,help)
                cmd="ltmatrix__help"
                ;;
            ltmatrix,man)
                cmd="ltmatrix__man"
                ;;
            ltmatrix,release)
                cmd="ltmatrix__release"
                ;;
            ltmatrix__help,cleanup)
                cmd="ltmatrix__help__cleanup"
                ;;
            ltmatrix__help,completions)
                cmd="ltmatrix__help__completions"
                ;;
            ltmatrix__help,help)
                cmd="ltmatrix__help__help"
                ;;
            ltmatrix__help,man)
                cmd="ltmatrix__help__man"
                ;;
            ltmatrix__help,release)
                cmd="ltmatrix__help__release"
                ;;
            *)
                ;;
        esac
    done

    case "${cmd}" in
        ltmatrix)
            opts="-c -h -V --agent --mode --fast --expert --config --output --log-level --log-file --max-retries --timeout --dry-run --resume --ask --regenerate-plan --on-blocked --mcp-config --no-color --help --version [GOAL] release completions man cleanup help"
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 1 ]] ; then
                COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                --agent)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0

                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W "fast standard expert" -- "${cur}"))
                    return 0

                    return 0

                    return 0
                    ;;
                --log-level)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W "trace debug info warn error" -- "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                --log-file)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0

                --max-retries)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))

            return 0
            ;;
        ltmatrix__cleanup)
            opts="-h --reset-all --reset-failed --remove --force --dry-run --no-color --help"
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 2 ]] ; then
                COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                *)
                    COMPREPLY=()
                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
            return 0
            ;;
        ltmatrix__completions)
            opts="-h --install --no-color --help bash zsh fish powershell elvish"
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 2 ]] ; then
                COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                *)
                    COMPREPLY=()
                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
            return 0

_ltmatrix() {
    local i cur prev opts cmd
    COMPREPLY=()
    if [[ "${BASH_VERSINFO[0]}" -ge 4 ]]; then
        cur="$2"
    else
        cur="${COMP_WORDS[COMP_CWORD]}"
    fi
    prev="$3"
    cmd=""
    opts=""

    for i in "${COMP_WORDS[@]:0:COMP_CWORD}"
    do
        case "${cmd},${i}" in
            ",$1")
                cmd="ltmatrix"
                ;;
            ltmatrix,cleanup)
                cmd="ltmatrix__cleanup"
                ;;
            ltmatrix,completions)
                cmd="ltmatrix__completions"
                ;;
            ltmatrix,help)
                cmd="ltmatrix__help"
                ;;
            ltmatrix,man)
                cmd="ltmatrix__man"
                ;;
            ltmatrix,release)
                cmd="ltmatrix__release"
                ;;
            ltmatrix__help,cleanup)
                cmd="ltmatrix__help__cleanup"
                ;;
            ltmatrix__help,completions)
                cmd="ltmatrix__help__completions"
                ;;
            ltmatrix__help,help)
                cmd="ltmatrix__help__help"
                ;;
            ltmatrix__help,man)
                cmd="ltmatrix__help__man"
                ;;
            ltmatrix__help,release)
                cmd="ltmatrix__help__release"
                ;;
            *)
                ;;
        esac
    done

    case "${cmd}" in
        ltmatrix)
            opts="-c -h -V --agent --mode --fast --expert --config --output --log-level --log-file --max-retries --timeout --dry-run --resume --ask --regenerate-plan --on-blocked --mcp-config --no-color --help --version [GOAL] release completions man cleanup help"
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 1 ]] ; then
                COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                --agent)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                --mode)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W "fast standard expert" -- "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                --config)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                -c)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                --output)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W "text json json-compact" -- "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                --log-level)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W "trace debug info warn error" -- "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                --log-file)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                --max-retries)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                --timeout)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                --on-blocked)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W "skip ask abort retry" -- "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                --mcp-config)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                *)
                    COMPREPLY=()
                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
            return 0
            ;;
        ltmatrix__cleanup)
            opts="-h --reset-all --reset-failed --remove --force --dry-run --no-color --help"
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 2 ]] ; then
                COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                *)
                    COMPREPLY=()
                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
            return 0
            ;;
        ltmatrix__completions)
            opts="-h --install --no-color --help bash zsh fish powershell elvish"
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 2 ]] ; then
                COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                *)
                    COMPREPLY=()
                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
            return 0
            ;;
        ltmatrix__help)
            opts="release completions man cleanup help"
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 2 ]] ; then
                COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                *)
                    COMPREPLY=()
                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
            return 0
            ;;
        ltmatrix__help__cleanup)
            opts=""
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 3 ]] ; then
                COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                *)
                    COMPREPLY=()
                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
            return 0
            ;;
        ltmatrix__help__completions)
            opts=""
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 3 ]] ; then
                COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                *)
                    COMPREPLY=()
                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
            return 0
            ;;
        ltmatrix__help__help)
            opts=""
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 3 ]] ; then
                COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                *)
                    COMPREPLY=()
                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
            return 0
            ;;
        ltmatrix__help__man)
            opts=""
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 3 ]] ; then
                COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                *)
                    COMPREPLY=()
                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
            return 0
            ;;
        ltmatrix__help__release)
            opts=""
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 3 ]] ; then
                COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                *)
                    COMPREPLY=()
                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
            return 0
            ;;
        ltmatrix__man)
            opts="-o -h --output --no-color --help"
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 2 ]] ; then
                COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                --output)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                -o)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                *)
                    COMPREPLY=()
                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
            return 0
            ;;
        ltmatrix__release)
            opts="-h --target --output --archive --all-targets --no-color --help"
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 2 ]] ; then
                COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                --target)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                --output)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                *)
                    COMPREPLY=()
                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
            return 0
            ;;
    esac
}

if [[ "${BASH_VERSINFO[0]}" -eq 4 && "${BASH_VERSINFO[1]}" -ge 4 || "${BASH_VERSINFO[0]}" -gt 4 ]]; then
    complete -F _ltmatrix -o nosort -o bashdefault -o default ltmatrix
else
    complete -F _ltmatrix -o bashdefault -o default ltmatrix
fi

                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
            return 0
            ;;
        ltmatrix__man)
            opts="-o -h --output --no-color --help"
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 2 ]] ; then
                COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                --output)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                -o)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                *)
                    COMPREPLY=()
                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
            return 0
            ;;
        ltmatrix__release)
            opts="-h --target --output --archive --all-targets --no-color --help"
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 2 ]] ; then
                COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                --target)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                --output)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                *)
                    COMPREPLY=()
                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
            return 0
            ;;
    esac
}

if [[ "${BASH_VERSINFO[0]}" -eq 4 && "${BASH_VERSINFO[1]}" -ge 4 || "${BASH_VERSINFO[0]}" -gt 4 ]]; then
    complete -F _ltmatrix -o nosort -o bashdefault -o default ltmatrix
else
    complete -F _ltmatrix -o bashdefault -o default ltmatrix
fi

#compdef ltmatrix

autoload -U is-at-least

_ltmatrix() {
    typeset -A opt_args
    typeset -a _arguments_options
    local ret=1

    if is-at-least 5.2; then
        _arguments_options=(-s -S -C)
    else
        _arguments_options=(-s -C)
    fi

    local context curcontext="$curcontext" state line
    _arguments "${_arguments_options[@]}" : \
'--agent=[Agent backend to use]:AGENT:_default' \
'--mode=[Execution mode preset]:MODE:(fast standard expert)' \
'-c+[Configuration file path]:FILE:_files' \
'--config=[Configuration file path]:FILE:_files' \
'--output=[Output format]:FORMAT:(text json json-compact)' \
'--log-level=[Log level]:LEVEL:(trace debug info warn error)' \
'--log-file=[Log file path]:FILE:_files' \
'--max-retries=[Maximum number of retries per task]:NUM:_default' \
'--timeout=[Timeout for operations (in seconds)]:SECONDS:_default' \
'--on-blocked=[Strategy for blocked tasks]:STRATEGY:(skip ask abort retry)' \
'--mcp-config=[MCP configuration file]:FILE:_files' \
'(--expert --mode)--fast[Fast execution mode]' \
'(--fast --mode)--expert[Expert execution mode]' \
'--dry-run[Generate plan without execution]' \
'--resume[Resume interrupted work]' \
'--ask[Ask for clarification before planning]' \
'--regenerate-plan[Regenerate the plan]' \
'--no-color[Disable colored output (respects NO_COLOR env var)]' \
'-h[Print help (see more with '\''--help'\'')]' \
'--help[Print help (see more with '\''--help'\'')]' \
'-V[Print version]' \
'--version[Print version]' \
'::goal -- The goal/task to accomplish:_default' \
":: :_ltmatrix_commands" \
"*::: :->ltmatrix" \
&& ret=0
    case $state in
    (ltmatrix)
        words=($line[2] "${words[@]}")
        (( CURRENT += 1 ))
        curcontext="${curcontext%:*:*}:ltmatrix-command-$line[2]:"
        case $line[2] in
            (release)
_arguments "${_arguments_options[@]}" : \
'--target=[Build target triple (e.g., x86_64-unknown-linux-musl)]:TRIPLE:_default' \
'--output=[Output directory for release artifacts]:DIR:_files' \
'--archive[Create release archives (tar.gz, zip)]' \
'--all-targets[Build for all supported targets]' \
'--no-color[Disable colored output (respects NO_COLOR env var)]' \
'-h[Print help]' \
'--help[Print help]' \
&& ret=0
;;
(completions)
_arguments "${_arguments_options[@]}" : \
'--install[Print installation instructions for the specified shell]' \
'--no-color[Disable colored output (respects NO_COLOR env var)]' \
'-h[Print help]' \
'--help[Print help]' \
':shell -- Shell type to generate completions for:(bash zsh fish powershell elvish)' \
&& ret=0
;;
(man)
_arguments "${_arguments_options[@]}" : \
'-o+[Output directory for man pages]:DIR:_files' \
'--output=[Output directory for man pages]:DIR:_files' \
'--no-color[Disable colored output (respects NO_COLOR env var)]' \
'-h[Print help]' \
'--help[Print help]' \
&& ret=0
;;
(cleanup)
_arguments "${_arguments_options[@]}" : \
'(--reset-failed)--reset-all[Reset all tasks to pending status (keeps state file)]' \
'--reset-failed[Reset only failed tasks to pending status (keeps state file)]' \
'(--reset-all --reset-failed)--remove[Remove all workspace state files]' \
'--force[Force cleanup without confirmation]' \
'--dry-run[Show what would be cleaned up without actually doing it]' \
'--no-color[Disable colored output (respects NO_COLOR env var)]' \
'-h[Print help]' \
'--help[Print help]' \
&& ret=0
;;
(help)
_arguments "${_arguments_options[@]}" : \
":: :_ltmatrix__help_commands" \
"*::: :->help" \
&& ret=0

    case $state in
    (help)
        words=($line[1] "${words[@]}")
        (( CURRENT += 1 ))
        curcontext="${curcontext%:*:*}:ltmatrix-help-command-$line[1]:"
        case $line[1] in
            (release)
_arguments "${_arguments_options[@]}" : \
&& ret=0
;;
(completions)
_arguments "${_arguments_options[@]}" : \
&& ret=0
;;
(man)
_arguments "${_arguments_options[@]}" : \
&& ret=0
;;
(cleanup)
_arguments "${_arguments_options[@]}" : \
&& ret=0
;;
(help)
_arguments "${_arguments_options[@]}" : \
&& ret=0
;;
        esac
    ;;
esac
;;
        esac
    ;;
esac
}

(( $+functions[_ltmatrix_commands] )) ||
_ltmatrix_commands() {
    local commands; commands=(
'release:Create a release build for distribution' \
'completions:Generate shell completion scripts' \
'man:Generate man pages' \
'cleanup:Clean up workspace state' \
'help:Print this message or the help of the given subcommand(s)' \
    )
    _describe -t commands 'ltmatrix commands' commands "$@"
}

    local commands; commands=()
    _describe -t commands 'ltmatrix cleanup commands' commands "$@"

}

# Print an optspec for argparse to handle cmd's options that are independent of any subcommand.
function __fish_ltmatrix_global_optspecs
	string join \n agent= mode= fast expert c/config= output= log-level= log-file= max-retries= timeout= dry-run resume ask regenerate-plan on-blocked= mcp-config= no-color h/help V/version
end

function __fish_ltmatrix_needs_command
	# Figure out if the current invocation already has a command.
	set -l cmd (commandline -opc)
	set -e cmd[1]
	argparse -s (__fish_ltmatrix_global_optspecs) -- $cmd 2>/dev/null
	or return
	if set -q argv[1]
		# Also print the command, so this can be used to figure out what it is.
		echo $argv[1]
		return 1
	end
	return 0
end

function __fish_ltmatrix_using_subcommand
	set -l cmd (__fish_ltmatrix_needs_command)
	test -z "$cmd"
	and return 1
	contains -- $cmd[1] $argv
end

using namespace System.Management.Automation
using namespace System.Management.Automation.Language

Register-ArgumentCompleter -Native -CommandName 'ltmatrix' -ScriptBlock {
    param($wordToComplete, $commandAst, $cursorPosition)

    $commandElements = $commandAst.CommandElements
    $command = @(
        'ltmatrix'
        for ($i = 1; $i -lt $commandElements.Count; $i++) {
            $element = $commandElements[$i]
            if ($element -isnot [StringConstantExpressionAst] -or
                $element.StringConstantType -ne [StringConstantType]::BareWord -or
                $element.Value.StartsWith('-') -or
                $element.Value -eq $wordToComplete) {
                break
        }
        $element.Value
    }) -join ';'

    $completions = @(switch ($command) {
        'ltmatrix' {
            [CompletionResult]::new('--agent', '--agent', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterName, 'Agent backend to use')
            [CompletionResult]::new('--mode', '--mode', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterName, 'Execution mode preset')
            [CompletionResult]::new('-c', '-c', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterName, 'Configuration file path')
            [CompletionResult]::new('--config', '--config', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterName, 'Configuration file path')
            [CompletionResult]::new('--output', '--output', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterName, 'Output format')
            [CompletionResult]::new('--log-level', '--log-level', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterName, 'Log level')
            [CompletionResult]::new('--log-file', '--log-file', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterName, 'Log file path')
            [CompletionResult]::new('--max-retries', '--max-retries', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterName, 'Maximum number of retries per task')
            [CompletionResult]::new('--timeout', '--timeout', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterName, 'Timeout for operations (in seconds)')
            [CompletionResult]::new('--on-blocked', '--on-blocked', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterName, 'Strategy for blocked tasks')
            [CompletionResult]::new('--mcp-config', '--mcp-config', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterName, 'MCP configuration file')
            [CompletionResult]::new('--fast', '--fast', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterName, 'Fast execution mode')
            [CompletionResult]::new('--expert', '--expert', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterName, 'Expert execution mode')
            [CompletionResult]::new('--dry-run', '--dry-run', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterName, 'Generate plan without execution')
            [CompletionResult]::new('--resume', '--resume', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterName, 'Resume interrupted work')
            [CompletionResult]::new('--ask', '--ask', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterName, 'Ask for clarification before planning')
            [CompletionResult]::new('--regenerate-plan', '--regenerate-plan', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterName, 'Regenerate the plan')
            [CompletionResult]::new('--no-color', '--no-color', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterName, 'Disable colored output (respects NO_COLOR env var)')
            [CompletionResult]::new('-h', '-h', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterName, 'Print help (see more with ''--help'')')
            [CompletionResult]::new('--help', '--help', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterName, 'Print help (see more with ''--help'')')
            [CompletionResult]::new('-V', '-V ', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterName, 'Print version')
            [CompletionResult]::new('--version', '--version', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterName, 'Print version')
            [CompletionResult]::new('release', 'release', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterValue, 'Create a release build for distribution')
            [CompletionResult]::new('completions', 'completions', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterValue, 'Generate shell completion scripts')
            [CompletionResult]::new('man', 'man', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterValue, 'Generate man pages')
            [CompletionResult]::new('cleanup', 'cleanup', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterValue, 'Clean up workspace state')
            [CompletionResult]::new('help', 'help', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterValue, 'Print this message or the help of the given subcommand(s)')
            break
        }
        'ltmatrix;release' {
            [CompletionResult]::new('--target', '--target', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterName, 'Build target triple (e.g., x86_64-unknown-linux-musl)')
            [CompletionResult]::new('--output', '--output', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterName, 'Output directory for release artifacts')
            [CompletionResult]::new('--archive', '--archive', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterName, 'Create release archives (tar.gz, zip)')
            [CompletionResult]::new('--all-targets', '--all-targets', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterName, 'Build for all supported targets')
            [CompletionResult]::new('--no-color', '--no-color', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterName, 'Disable colored output (respects NO_COLOR env var)')
            [CompletionResult]::new('-h', '-h', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterName, 'Print help')
            [CompletionResult]::new('--help', '--help', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterName, 'Print help')
            break
        }
        'ltmatrix;completions' {
            [CompletionResult]::new('--install', '--install', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterName, 'Print installation instructions for the specified shell')
            [CompletionResult]::new('--no-color', '--no-color', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterName, 'Disable colored output (respects NO_COLOR env var)')
            [CompletionResult]::new('-h', '-h', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterName, 'Print help')
            [CompletionResult]::new('--help', '--help', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterName, 'Print help')
            break
        }
        'ltmatrix;man' {
            [CompletionResult]::new('-o', '-o', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterName, 'Output directory for man pages')
            [CompletionResult]::new('--output', '--output', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterName, 'Output directory for man pages')
            [CompletionResult]::new('--no-color', '--no-color', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterName, 'Disable colored output (respects NO_COLOR env var)')
            [CompletionResult]::new('-h', '-h', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterName, 'Print help')
            [CompletionResult]::new('--help', '--help', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterName, 'Print help')
            break
        }
        'ltmatrix;cleanup' {
            [CompletionResult]::new('--reset-all', '--reset-all', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterName, 'Reset all tasks to pending status (keeps state file)')
            [CompletionResult]::new('--reset-failed', '--reset-failed', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterName, 'Reset only failed tasks to pending status (keeps state file)')
            [CompletionResult]::new('--remove', '--remove', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterName, 'Remove all workspace state files')
            [CompletionResult]::new('--force', '--force', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterName, 'Force cleanup without confirmation')
            [CompletionResult]::new('--dry-run', '--dry-run', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterName, 'Show what would be cleaned up without actually doing it')
            [CompletionResult]::new('--no-color', '--no-color', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterName, 'Disable colored output (respects NO_COLOR env var)')
            [CompletionResult]::new('-h', '-h', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterName, 'Print help')
            [CompletionResult]::new('--help', '--help', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterName, 'Print help')
            break
        }
        'ltmatrix;help' {
            [CompletionResult]::new('release', 'release', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterValue, 'Create a release build for distribution')
            [CompletionResult]::new('completions', 'completions', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterValue, 'Generate shell completion scripts')
            [CompletionResult]::new('man', 'man', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterValue, 'Generate man pages')
            [CompletionResult]::new('cleanup', 'cleanup', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterValue, 'Clean up workspace state')
            [CompletionResult]::new('help', 'help', [CompletionResultType]::ParameterValue, 'Print this message or the help of the given subcommand(s)')
            break
        }
        'ltmatrix;help;release' {
            break
        }
        'ltmatrix;help;completions' {
            break
        }
        'ltmatrix;help;man' {
            break
        }
        'ltmatrix;help;cleanup' {
            break
        }
        'ltmatrix;help;help' {
            break
        }
    })

    $completions.Where{ $_.CompletionText -like "$wordToComplete*" } |
        Sort-Object -Property ListItemText
}
test test_invalid_blocked_strategy ... ok
test test_log_level_display ... ok

use builtin;
use str;

set edit:completion:arg-completer[ltmatrix] = {|@words|
    fn spaces {|n|
        builtin:repeat $n ' ' | str:join ''
    }
    fn cand {|text desc|
        edit:complex-candidate $text &display=$text' '(spaces (- 14 (wcswidth $text)))$desc
    }
    var command = 'ltmatrix'
    for word $words[1..-1] {
        if (str:has-prefix $word '-') {
            break
        }
        set command = $command';'$word
    }
    var completions = [
        &'ltmatrix'= {
            cand --agent 'Agent backend to use'
            cand --mode 'Execution mode preset'
            cand -c 'Configuration file path'
            cand --config 'Configuration file path'
            cand --output 'Output format'
            cand --log-level 'Log level'
            cand --log-file 'Log file path'
            cand --max-retries 'Maximum number of retries per task'
            cand --timeout 'Timeout for operations (in seconds)'
            cand --on-blocked 'Strategy for blocked tasks'
            cand --mcp-config 'MCP configuration file'
            cand --fast 'Fast execution mode'
            cand --expert 'Expert execution mode'
            cand --dry-run 'Generate plan without execution'
            cand --resume 'Resume interrupted work'
            cand --ask 'Ask for clarification before planning'
            cand --regenerate-plan 'Regenerate the plan'
            cand --no-color 'Disable colored output (respects NO_COLOR env var)'
            cand -h 'Print help (see more with ''--help'')'
            cand --help 'Print help (see more with ''--help'')'
            cand -V 'Print version'
            cand --version 'Print version'
            cand release 'Create a release build for distribution'
            cand completions 'Generate shell completion scripts'
            cand man 'Generate man pages'
            cand cleanup 'Clean up workspace state'
            cand help 'Print this message or the help of the given subcommand(s)'
        }
        &'ltmatrix;release'= {
            cand --target 'Build target triple (e.g., x86_64-unknown-linux-musl)'
            cand --output 'Output directory for release artifacts'
            cand --archive 'Create release archives (tar.gz, zip)'
            cand --all-targets 'Build for all supported targets'
            cand --no-color 'Disable colored output (respects NO_COLOR env var)'
            cand -h 'Print help'
            cand --help 'Print help'
        }
        &'ltmatrix;completions'= {
            cand --install 'Print installation instructions for the specified shell'
            cand --no-color 'Disable colored output (respects NO_COLOR env var)'
            cand -h 'Print help'
            cand --help 'Print help'
        }
        &'ltmatrix;man'= {
            cand -o 'Output directory for man pages'
            cand --output 'Output directory for man pages'
            cand --no-color 'Disable colored output (respects NO_COLOR env var)'
            cand -h 'Print help'
            cand --help 'Print help'
        }
        &'ltmatrix;cleanup'= {
            cand --reset-all 'Reset all tasks to pending status (keeps state file)'
            cand --reset-failed 'Reset only failed tasks to pending status (keeps state file)'
            cand --remove 'Remove all workspace state files'
            cand --force 'Force cleanup without confirmation'
            cand --dry-run 'Show what would be cleaned up without actually doing it'
            cand --no-color 'Disable colored output (respects NO_COLOR env var)'
            cand -h 'Print help'
            cand --help 'Print help'
        }
        &'ltmatrix;help'= {
            cand release 'Create a release build for distribution'
            cand completions 'Generate shell completion scripts'
            cand man 'Generate man pages'
            cand cleanup 'Clean up workspace state'
            cand help 'Print this message or the help of the given subcommand(s)'
        }
        &'ltmatrix;help;release'= {
        }
        &'ltmatrix;help;completions'= {
        }
        &'ltmatrix;help;man'= {
        }
        &'ltmatrix;help;cleanup'= {
        }
        &'ltmatrix;help;help'= {
        }
    ]
    $completions[$command]
}

_ltmatrix() {
    local i cur prev opts cmd
    COMPREPLY=()
    if [[ "${BASH_VERSINFO[0]}" -ge 4 ]]; then
        cur="$2"
    else
        cur="${COMP_WORDS[COMP_CWORD]}"
    fi
    prev="$3"
    cmd=""
    opts=""

    for i in "${COMP_WORDS[@]:0:COMP_CWORD}"
    do
        case "${cmd},${i}" in
            ",$1")
                cmd="ltmatrix"
                ;;
            ltmatrix,cleanup)
                cmd="ltmatrix__cleanup"
                ;;
            ltmatrix,completions)
                cmd="ltmatrix__completions"
                ;;
            ltmatrix,help)
                cmd="ltmatrix__help"
                ;;
            ltmatrix,man)
                cmd="ltmatrix__man"
                ;;
            ltmatrix,release)
                cmd="ltmatrix__release"
                ;;
            ltmatrix__help,cleanup)
                cmd="ltmatrix__help__cleanup"
                ;;
            ltmatrix__help,completions)
                cmd="ltmatrix__help__completions"
                ;;
            ltmatrix__help,help)
                cmd="ltmatrix__help__help"
                ;;
            ltmatrix__help,man)
                cmd="ltmatrix__help__man"
                ;;
            ltmatrix__help,release)
                cmd="ltmatrix__help__release"
                ;;
            *)
                ;;
        esac
    done

    case "${cmd}" in
        ltmatrix)
            opts="-c -h -V --agent --mode --fast --expert --config --output --log-level --log-file --max-retries --timeout --dry-run --resume --ask --regenerate-plan --on-blocked --mcp-config --no-color --help --version [GOAL] release completions man cleanup help"
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 1 ]] ; then
                COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                --agent)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                --mode)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W "fast standard expert" -- "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                --config)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                -c)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                --output)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W "text json json-compact" -- "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                --log-level)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W "trace debug info warn error" -- "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                --log-file)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                --max-retries)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                --timeout)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                --on-blocked)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W "skip ask abort retry" -- "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                --mcp-config)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                *)
                    COMPREPLY=()
                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
            return 0
            ;;
        ltmatrix__cleanup)
            opts="-h --reset-all --reset-failed --remove --force --dry-run --no-color --help"
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 2 ]] ; then
                COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                *)
                    COMPREPLY=()
                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
            return 0
            ;;
        ltmatrix__completions)
            opts="-h --install --no-color --help bash zsh fish powershell elvish"
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 2 ]] ; then
                COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                *)
                    COMPREPLY=()
                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
            return 0
            ;;
        ltmatrix__help)
            opts="release completions man cleanup help"
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 2 ]] ; then
                COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                *)
                    COMPREPLY=()
                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
            return 0
            ;;
        ltmatrix__help__cleanup)
            opts=""
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 3 ]] ; then
                COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                *)
                    COMPREPLY=()
                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
            return 0
            ;;
        ltmatrix__help__completions)
            opts=""
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 3 ]] ; then
                COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                *)
                    COMPREPLY=()
                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
            return 0
            ;;
        ltmatrix__help__help)
            opts=""
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 3 ]] ; then
                COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                *)
                    COMPREPLY=()
                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
            return 0
            ;;
        ltmatrix__help__man)
            opts=""
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 3 ]] ; then
                COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                *)
                    COMPREPLY=()
                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
            return 0
            ;;
        ltmatrix__help__release)
            opts=""
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 3 ]] ; then
                COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                *)
                    COMPREPLY=()
                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
            return 0
            ;;
        ltmatrix__man)
            opts="-o -h --output --no-color --help"
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 2 ]] ; then
                COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                --output)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                -o)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                *)
                    COMPREPLY=()
                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
            return 0
            ;;
        ltmatrix__release)
            opts="-h --target --output --archive --all-targets --no-color --help"
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 2 ]] ; then
                COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                --target)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                --output)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                *)
                    COMPREPLY=()
                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
            return 0
            ;;
    esac
}

if [[ "${BASH_VERSINFO[0]}" -eq 4 && "${BASH_VERSINFO[1]}" -ge 4 || "${BASH_VERSINFO[0]}" -gt 4 ]]; then
    complete -F _ltmatrix -o nosort -o bashdefault -o default ltmatrix
else
    complete -F _ltmatrix -o bashdefault -o default ltmatrix
fi

            opts=""
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 3 ]] ; then
                COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                *)
                    COMPREPLY=()
                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
            return 0
            ;;
        ltmatrix__help__completions)
            opts=""
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 3 ]] ; then
                COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                *)
                    COMPREPLY=()
                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
            return 0
            ;;
        ltmatrix__help__help)
            opts=""
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 3 ]] ; then
                COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                *)
                    COMPREPLY=()
                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
            return 0
            ;;
        ltmatrix__help__man)
            opts=""
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 3 ]] ; then
                COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                *)
                    COMPREPLY=()
                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
            return 0
            ;;
        ltmatrix__help__release)
            opts=""
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 3 ]] ; then
                COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                *)
                    COMPREPLY=()
                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
            return 0
            ;;
        ltmatrix__man)
            opts="-o -h --output --no-color --help"
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 2 ]] ; then
                COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                --output)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                -o)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                *)
                    COMPREPLY=()
                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
            return 0
            ;;
        ltmatrix__release)
            opts="-h --target --output --archive --all-targets --no-color --help"
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 2 ]] ; then
                COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                --target)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                --output)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                *)
                    COMPREPLY=()
                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
            return 0
            ;;
    esac
}

if [[ "${BASH_VERSINFO[0]}" -eq 4 && "${BASH_VERSINFO[1]}" -ge 4 || "${BASH_VERSINFO[0]}" -gt 4 ]]; then
    complete -F _ltmatrix -o nosort -o bashdefault -o default ltmatrix
else
    complete -F _ltmatrix -o bashdefault -o default ltmatrix
fi
test test_completion_includes_version_flag ... ok
test test_completion_with_special_characters_in_command_name ... ok

_ltmatrix() {
    local i cur prev opts cmd
    COMPREPLY=()
    if [[ "${BASH_VERSINFO[0]}" -ge 4 ]]; then
        cur="$2"
    else
        cur="${COMP_WORDS[COMP_CWORD]}"
    fi
    prev="$3"
    cmd=""
    opts=""

    for i in "${COMP_WORDS[@]:0:COMP_CWORD}"
    do
        case "${cmd},${i}" in
            ",$1")
                cmd="ltmatrix"
                ;;
            ltmatrix,cleanup)
                cmd="ltmatrix__cleanup"
                ;;
            ltmatrix,completions)
                cmd="ltmatrix__completions"
                ;;
            ltmatrix,help)
                cmd="ltmatrix__help"
                ;;
            ltmatrix,man)
                cmd="ltmatrix__man"
                ;;
            ltmatrix,release)
                cmd="ltmatrix__release"
                ;;
            ltmatrix__help,cleanup)
                cmd="ltmatrix__help__cleanup"
                ;;
            ltmatrix__help,completions)
                cmd="ltmatrix__help__completions"
                ;;
            ltmatrix__help,help)
                cmd="ltmatrix__help__help"
                ;;
            ltmatrix__help,man)
                cmd="ltmatrix__help__man"
                ;;
            ltmatrix__help,release)
                cmd="ltmatrix__help__release"
                ;;
            *)
                ;;
        esac
    done

    case "${cmd}" in
        ltmatrix)
            opts="-c -h -V --agent --mode --fast --expert --config --output --log-level --log-file --max-retries --timeout --dry-run --resume --ask --regenerate-plan --on-blocked --mcp-config --no-color --help --version [GOAL] release completions man cleanup help"
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 1 ]] ; then
                COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                --agent)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                --mode)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W "fast standard expert" -- "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                --config)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                -c)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                --output)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W "text json json-compact" -- "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                --log-level)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W "trace debug info warn error" -- "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                --log-file)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                --max-retries)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                --timeout)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                --on-blocked)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W "skip ask abort retry" -- "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                --mcp-config)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                *)
                    COMPREPLY=()
                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
            return 0
            ;;
        ltmatrix__cleanup)
            opts="-h --reset-all --reset-failed --remove --force --dry-run --no-color --help"
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 2 ]] ; then
                COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                *)
                    COMPREPLY=()
                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
            return 0
            ;;
        ltmatrix__completions)
            opts="-h --install --no-color --help bash zsh fish powershell elvish"
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 2 ]] ; then
                COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                *)
                    COMPREPLY=()
                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
            return 0
            ;;
        ltmatrix__help)
            opts="release completions man cleanup help"
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 2 ]] ; then
                COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                *)
                    COMPREPLY=()
                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
            return 0
            ;;
        ltmatrix__help__cleanup)
            opts=""
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 3 ]] ; then
                COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                *)
                    COMPREPLY=()
                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
            return 0
            ;;
        ltmatrix__help__completions)
            opts=""
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 3 ]] ; then
                COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                *)
                    COMPREPLY=()
                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
            return 0
            ;;
        ltmatrix__help__help)
            opts=""
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 3 ]] ; then
                COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                *)
                    COMPREPLY=()
                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
            return 0
            ;;
        ltmatrix__help__man)
            opts=""
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 3 ]] ; then
                COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                *)
                    COMPREPLY=()
                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
            return 0
            ;;
        ltmatrix__help__release)
            opts=""
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 3 ]] ; then
                COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                *)
                    COMPREPLY=()
                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
            return 0
            ;;
        ltmatrix__man)
            opts="-o -h --output --no-color --help"
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 2 ]] ; then
                COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                --output)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                -o)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                *)
                    COMPREPLY=()
                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
            return 0
            ;;
        ltmatrix__release)
            opts="-h --target --output --archive --all-targets --no-color --help"
            if [[ ${cur} == -* || ${COMP_CWORD} -eq 2 ]] ; then
                COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
                return 0
            fi
            case "${prev}" in
                --target)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                --output)
                    COMPREPLY=($(compgen -f "${cur}"))
                    return 0
                    ;;
                *)
                    COMPREPLY=()
                    ;;
            esac
            COMPREPLY=( $(compgen -W "${opts}" -- "${cur}") )
            return 0
            ;;
    esac
}

use builtin;
use str;

set edit:completion:arg-completer[ltmatrix] = {|@words|
    fn spaces {|n|
        builtin:repeat $n ' ' | str:join ''
    }
    fn cand {|text desc|
        edit:complex-candidate $text &display=$text' '(spaces (- 14 (wcswidth $text)))$desc
    }
    var command = 'ltmatrix'
    for word $words[1..-1] {
        if (str:has-prefix $word '-') {
            break
        }
        set command = $command';'$word
    }
    var completions = [
        &'ltmatrix'= {
            cand --agent 'Agent backend to use'
            cand --mode 'Execution mode preset'
            cand -c 'Configuration file path'
            cand --config 'Configuration file path'
            cand --output 'Output format'
            cand --log-level 'Log level'
            cand --log-file 'Log file path'
            cand --max-retries 'Maximum number of retries per task'
            cand --timeout 'Timeout for operations (in seconds)'
            cand --on-blocked 'Strategy for blocked tasks'
            cand --mcp-config 'MCP configuration file'
            cand --fast 'Fast execution mode'
            cand --expert 'Expert execution mode'
            cand --dry-run 'Generate plan without execution'
            cand --resume 'Resume interrupted work'
            cand --ask 'Ask for clarification before planning'
            cand --regenerate-plan 'Regenerate the plan'
            cand --no-color 'Disable colored output (respects NO_COLOR env var)'
            cand -h 'Print help (see more with ''--help'')'
            cand --help 'Print help (see more with ''--help'')'
            cand -V 'Print version'
            cand --version 'Print version'
            cand release 'Create a release build for distribution'
            cand completions 'Generate shell completion scripts'
            cand man 'Generate man pages'
            cand cleanup 'Clean up workspace state'
            cand help 'Print this message or the help of the given subcommand(s)'
        }
        &'ltmatrix;release'= {
            cand --target 'Build target triple (e.g., x86_64-unknown-linux-musl)'
            cand --output 'Output directory for release artifacts'
            cand --archive 'Create release archives (tar.gz, zip)'
            cand --all-targets 'Build for all supported targets'
            cand --no-color 'Disable colored output (respects NO_COLOR env var)'
            cand -h 'Print help'
            cand --help 'Print help'
        }
        &'ltmatrix;completions'= {
            cand --install 'Print installation instructions for the specified shell'
            cand --no-color 'Disable colored output (respects NO_COLOR env var)'
            cand -h 'Print help'
            cand --help 'Print help'
        }
        &'ltmatrix;man'= {
            cand -o 'Output directory for man pages'
            cand --output 'Output directory for man pages'
            cand --no-color 'Disable colored output (respects NO_COLOR env var)'
            cand -h 'Print help'
            cand --help 'Print help'
        }
        &'ltmatrix;cleanup'= {
            cand --reset-all 'Reset all tasks to pending status (keeps state file)'
            cand --reset-failed 'Reset only failed tasks to pending status (keeps state file)'
            cand --remove 'Remove all workspace state files'
            cand --force 'Force cleanup without confirmation'
            cand --dry-run 'Show what would be cleaned up without actually doing it'
            cand --no-color 'Disable colored output (respects NO_COLOR env var)'
            cand -h 'Print help'
            cand --help 'Print help'
        }
        &'ltmatrix;help'= {
            cand release 'Create a release build for distribution'
            cand completions 'Generate shell completion scripts'
            cand man 'Generate man pages'
            cand cleanup 'Clean up workspace state'
            cand help 'Print this message or the help of the given subcommand(s)'
        }
        &'ltmatrix;help;release'= {
        }
        &'ltmatrix;help;completions'= {
        }
        &'ltmatrix;help;man'= {
        }
        &'ltmatrix;help;cleanup'= {
        }
        &'ltmatrix;help;help'= {
        }
    ]
    $completions[$command]
}

# Print an optspec for argparse to handle cmd's options that are independent of any subcommand.
function __fish_ltmatrix_global_optspecs
	string join \n agent= mode= fast expert c/config= output= log-level= log-file= max-retries= timeout= dry-run resume ask regenerate-plan on-blocked= mcp-config= no-color h/help V/version
end

function __fish_ltmatrix_needs_command
	# Figure out if the current invocation already has a command.
	set -l cmd (commandline -opc)
	set -e cmd[1]
	argparse -s (__fish_ltmatrix_global_optspecs) -- $cmd 2>/dev/null
	or return
	if set -q argv[1]
		# Also print the command, so this can be used to figure out what it is.
		echo $argv[1]
		return 1
	end
	return 0
end

function __fish_ltmatrix_using_subcommand
	set -l cmd (__fish_ltmatrix_needs_command)
	test -z "$cmd"
	and return 1
	contains -- $cmd[1] $argv
end
